# <a name="search-the-audit-log-in-the-security--compliance-center"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-103">在安全性與合規性中心搜尋稽核記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-103">Search the audit log in the Security & Compliance Center</span></span>

## <a name="introduction"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-104">簡介</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-104">Introduction</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-105">需要了解是否有使用者已檢視特定文件或清除信箱中的項目嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-105">Need to find if a user viewed a specific document or purged an item from their mailbox?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-106">如果是，您可以使用 Office 365 安全性與合規性中心來搜尋統一的稽核記錄，檢視 Office 365 組織中的使用者和系統管理員活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-106">If so, you can use the Office 365 Security & Compliance Center to search the unified audit log to view user and administrator activity in your Office 365 organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-107">為什麼使用整合的稽核記錄？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-107">Why a unified audit log?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-108">因為您可以在 Office 365 中搜尋下列類型的使用者和系統管理員活動：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-108">Because you can search for the following types of user and admin activity in Office 365:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-109">SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中的使用者活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-109">User activity in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-110">Exchange Online 中的使用者活動 (Exchange 信箱稽核記錄)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-110">User activity in Exchange Online (Exchange mailbox audit logging)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-111">SharePoint Online 中的系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-111">Admin activity in SharePoint Online</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-112">Azure Active Directory (適用於 Office 365 的目錄服務) 中的系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-112">Admin activity in Azure Active Directory (the directory service for Office 365)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-113">Exchange Online 中的系統管理員活動 (Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-113">Admin activity in Exchange Online (Exchange admin audit logging)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-114">Sway 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-114">User and admin activity in Sway</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-115">安全性與合規性中心中的電子文件探索活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-115">eDiscovery activities in the security and compliance center</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-116">Power BI 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-116">User and admin activity in Power BI</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-117">Microsoft Teams 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-117">User and admin activity in Microsoft Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-118">Dynamics 365 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-118">User and admin activity in Dynamics 365</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-119">Yammer 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-119">User and admin activity in Yammer</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-120">Microsoft Power Automate 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-120">User and admin activity in Microsoft Power Automate</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-121">Microsoft Stream 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-121">User and admin activity in Microsoft Stream</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-122">Microsoft 工作場所分析中的分析師和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-122">Analyst and admin activity in Microsoft Workplace Analytics</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-123">Microsoft Power Apps 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-123">User and admin activity in Microsoft Power Apps</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-124">Microsoft Flow 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-124">User and admin activity in Microsoft Forms</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-125">使用 SharePoint Online 或 Microsoft Teams 網站之敏感度標籤的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-125">User and admin activity for sensitivity labels for sites that use SharePoint Online or Microsoft Teams</span></span>

## <a name="before-you-begin"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-126">開始之前</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-126">Before you begin</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-127">在您開始搜尋 Office 365 稽核記錄前，請務必閱讀下列項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-127">Be sure to read the following items before you start searching the Office 365 audit log.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-128">您 (或其他系統管理員) 必須先開啟稽核記錄，才能開始搜尋 Office 365 稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-128">You (or another admin) must first turn on audit logging before you can start searching the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-129">按一下「安全性與合規性中心」中 **[稽核記錄搜尋]** 頁面上的 **[開啟稽核]**，即可開啟此功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-129">To turn it on, click **Turn on auditing** on the **Audit log search** page in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-130">(如果您沒看到此連結，表示您的組織已開啟稽核功能。) 開啟此功能後，就會顯示一則訊息，表示正在準備稽核記錄，而您可以在準備完成 (約幾小時) 後執行搜尋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-130">(If you don't see this link, auditing has already been turned on for your organization.) After you turn it on, a message is displayed that says the audit log is being prepared and that you can run a search in a couple of hours after the preparation is complete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-131">此操作只需執行一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-131">You only have to do this once.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-132">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[開啟或關閉稽核記錄搜尋](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-132">For more information, see [Turn audit log search on or off](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md).</span></span>

  > [!NOTE]
  > <span data-ttu-id="078fd-133">我們還在設法讓稽核功能可預設為開啟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-133">We're in the process of turning on auditing by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-134">在那之前，您可以如上述方法來開啟該功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-134">Until then, you can turn it on as previously described.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-135">您必須在 Exchange Online 中獲派為 [僅限檢視稽核記錄] 或 [稽核記錄] 角色，才能搜尋 Office 365 稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-135">You have to be assigned the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role in Exchange Online to search the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-136">根據預設，這些角色會在 Exchange 系統管理員中心的 [權限]\*\*\*\* 頁面上，指派給 [法務遵循管理] 和 [組織管理] 角色群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-136">By default, these roles are assigned to the Compliance Management and Organization Management role groups on the **Permissions** page in the Exchange admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-137">請注意，Office 365 和 Microsoft 365 中的全域系統管理員會自動成為 Exchange Online 中 [組織管理] 角色群組的成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-137">Note Global administrators in Office 365 and Microsoft 365 are automatically added as members of the Organization Management role group in Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-138">若要提供使用者能夠搜尋 Office 365 稽核記錄的最低權限等級，您可以在 Exchange Online 中建立自訂角色群組、新增 [僅限檢視稽核記錄] 或 [稽核記錄] 角色，然後將使用者加入這個新的角色群組成為其中的成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-138">To give a user the ability to search the Office 365 audit log with the minimum level of privileges, you can create a custom role group in Exchange Online, add the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role, and then add the user as a member of the new role group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-139">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[管理 Exchange Online 中的角色群組](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=730688)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-139">For more information, see [Manage role groups in Exchange Online](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=730688).</span></span>

  > [!IMPORTANT]
  > <span data-ttu-id="078fd-140">如果您在安全性與合規性中心的 [權限]\*\*\*\* 頁面上，將 [僅限檢視稽核記錄] 或 [稽核記錄] 角色指派給使用者，使用者將無法搜尋 Office 365 稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-140">If you assign a user the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role on the **Permissions** page in the Security & Compliance Center, they won't be able to search the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-141">您必須在 Exchange Online 中指派權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-141">You have to assign the permissions in Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-142">這是因為用來搜尋稽核記錄的基礎 Cmdlet 是 Exchange Online Cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-142">This is because the underlying cmdlet used to search the audit log is an Exchange Online cmdlet.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-143">當使用者或系統管理員執行稽核的活動時，稽核記錄會隨即產生，並儲存在您組織的 Office 365 稽核記錄中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-143">When an audited activity is performed by a user or admin, an audit record is generated and stored in the Office 365 audit log for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-144">稽核記錄的保留時間及可在稽核記錄中搜尋的時間長度，取決於您的 Office 365 或 Microsoft 365 企業版訂閱，具體來說，取決於指派給特定使用者的授權類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-144">The length of time that an audit record is retained (and searchable in the audit log) depends on your Office 365 or Microsoft 365 enterprise subscription, and specifically the type of the license that is assigned to a specific user.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="078fd-145">**Office 365 E3 或 Microsoft 365 E3：** 稽核記錄會保留 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-145">**Office 365 E3 or Microsoft 365 E3:** Audit records are retained for 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-146">這表示您可以搜尋稽核記錄來尋找過去 90 天中執行的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-146">That means you can search the audit log for activities that were performed within the last 90 days.</span></span>

    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="078fd-147">即使信箱稽核預設為開啟，您可能會發現某些使用者的信箱稽核事件在安全性與合規性中心的稽核記錄搜尋或透過 Office 365 管理活動 API 找不到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-147">Even when mailbox auditing on by default is turned on, you might notice that mailbox audit events for some users aren't found in audit log searches in the Security & Compliance Center or via the Office 365 Management Activity API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-148">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[信箱稽核記錄的相關資訊](enable-mailbox-auditing.md#more-information)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-148">For more information, see [More information about mailbox audit logging](enable-mailbox-auditing.md#more-information).</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="078fd-149">**Office 365 E5 或 Microsoft 365 E5 或擁有 Microsoft 365 E5 合規性附加元件授權的使用者：** Azure Active Directory、Exchange 和 SharePoint 活動的稽核記錄依預設會保留一年。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-149">**Office 365 E5 or Microsoft 365 E5 or users with a Microsoft 365 E5 Compliance add-on license:** Audit records for Azure Active Directory, Exchange, and SharePoint activity are retained for one year by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-150">組織也可建立稽核記錄保留原則，以保留其他服務中的活動稽核記錄，最長一年。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-150">Organizations can also create audit log retention policies to retain audit records for activity in other services for up to one year.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-151">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[管理稽核記錄保留原則](audit-log-retention-policies.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-151">For more information, see [Manage audit log retention policies](audit-log-retention-policies.md).</span></span>

    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="078fd-152">如果您的組織有參與一年期稽核記錄保留的私人預覽計畫，則將不會重設一般發行日期之前產生的稽核記錄保留期間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-152">If your organization participated in the private preview program for the one-year retention of audit records, the retention duration for audit records that were generated before the general availability rollout date will not be reset.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-153">如果您想要關閉貴組織在 Office 365 中的稽核記錄搜尋功能，您可以在與 Exchange Online 組織連線的遠端 PowerShell 中執行下列命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-153">If you want to turn off audit log search in Office 365 for your organization, you can run the following command in remote PowerShell connected to your Exchange Online organization:</span></span>

  ```powershell
  Set-AdminAuditLogConfig -UnifiedAuditLogIngestionEnabled $false
  ```

    <span data-ttu-id="078fd-154">若要再次開啟稽核搜尋，您可以在 Exchange Online PowerShell 中執行下列命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-154">To turn on audit search again, you can run the following command in Exchange Online PowerShell:</span></span>

  ```powershell
  Set-AdminAuditLogConfig -UnifiedAuditLogIngestionEnabled $true
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="078fd-155">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[關閉 Office 365 中的稽核記錄搜尋](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-155">For more information, see [Turn off audit log search in Office 365](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-156">如先前所述，用來搜尋稽核記錄的基礎 Cmdlet 是 Exchange Online Cmdlet，也就是 **Search-UnifiedAuditLog**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-156">As previously stated, the underlying cmdlet used to search the audit log is an Exchange Online cmdlet, which is **Search-UnifiedAuditLog**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-157">這表示您可以使用此 Cmdlet 來搜尋 Office 365 稽核記錄，而不是使用安全性與合規性中心中的 [稽核記錄搜尋]\*\*\*\* 頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-157">That means you can use this cmdlet to search the Office 365 audit log instead of using the **Audit log search** page in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-158">您必須在連線到 Exchange Online 組織的遠端 PowerShell，執行此 Cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-158">You have to run this cmdlet in remote PowerShell connected to your Exchange Online organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-159">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [Search-UnifiedAuditLog](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=834776)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-159">For more information, see [Search-UnifiedAuditLog](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=834776).</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="078fd-160">若要了解如何將 **Search-UnifiedAuditLog** Cmdlet 所傳回的搜尋結果匯出為 CSV 檔案，請參閱[匯出、設定及檢視稽核記錄檔的記錄](export-view-audit-log-records.md#tips-for-exporting-and-viewing-the-audit-log)中的＜匯出及檢視稽核記錄的秘訣＞一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-160">For information about exporting the search results returned by the **Search-UnifiedAuditLog** cmdlet to a CSV file, see the "Tips for exporting and viewing the audit log" section in [Export, configure, and view audit log records](export-view-audit-log-records.md#tips-for-exporting-and-viewing-the-audit-log).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-161">如果您想要以程式設計方式從 Office 365 稽核記錄下載資料，我們建議您使用 Office 365 管理活動 API，而非使用 PowerShell 指令碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-161">If you want to programmatically download data from the Office 365 audit log, we recommend that you use the Office 365 Management Activity API instead of using a PowerShell script.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-162">Office 365 管理活動 API 是一個 REST Web 服務，可用於為貴組織開發作業、安全性以及合規性的監控解決方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-162">The Office 365 Management Activity API is a REST web service that you can use to develop operations, security, and compliance monitoring solutions for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-163">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [Office 365 管理活動 API 參考](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/office-365-management-activity-api-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-163">For more information, see [Office 365 Management Activity API reference](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/office-365-management-activity-api-reference).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-164">發生事件後，對應的稽核記錄最多可能需要 30 分鐘或 24 小時的時間，才會在稽核記錄搜尋的結果中傳回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-164">It can take up to 30 minutes or up to 24 hours after an event occurs for the corresponding audit log record to be returned in the results of an audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-165">下列表格顯示不同 Office 365 服務的所需時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-165">The following table shows the time it takes for the different services in Office 365.</span></span>

  |<span data-ttu-id="078fd-166">**Office 365 服務**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-166">**Office 365 service**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-167">**30 分鐘**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-167">**30 minutes**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-168">**24 小時**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-168">**24 hours**</span></span>|
  |:-----|:-----:|:-----:|
  |<span data-ttu-id="078fd-169">進階威脅防護和威脅情報</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-169">Advanced Threat Protection and Threat Intelligence</span></span>|![核取記號](../media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)||
  |<span data-ttu-id="078fd-171">Azure Active Directory (使用者登入活動)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-171">Azure Active Directory (user login events)</span></span>||![核取記號](../media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)|
  |<span data-ttu-id="078fd-173">Azure Active Directory (系統管理員活動)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-173">Azure Active Directory (admin events)</span></span>||![核取記號](../media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)|

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-207">Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) 是適用於 Office 365 的目錄服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-207">Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) is the directory service for Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-208">整合的稽核記錄包含 Microsoft 365 系統管理員中心或 Azure 管理入口網站中執行的使用者、群組、應用程式、網域及目錄活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-208">The unified audit log contains user, group, application, domain, and directory activities performed in the Microsoft 365 admin center or in the Azure management portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-209">如需 Azure AD 事件的完整清單，請參閱 [Azure Active Directory 稽核報告事件](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=616549)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-209">For a complete list of Azure AD events, see [Azure Active Directory Audit Report Events](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=616549).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-210">Power BI 的稽核記錄未預設為啟用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-210">Audit logging for Power BI isn't enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-211">若要在 Office 365 稽核記錄中搜尋 Power BI 活動，您必須在 Power BI 系統管理入口網站中啟用稽核功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-211">To search for Power BI activities in the Office 365 audit log, you have to enable auditing in the Power BI admin portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-212">如需相關指示，請參閱 [Power BI 系統管理員入口網站](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs)中的＜稽核記錄＞一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-212">For instructions, see the "Audit logs" section in [Power BI admin portal](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs).</span></span>

## <a name="search-the-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-213">搜尋稽核記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-213">Search the audit log</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-214">下列是在 Office 365 中搜尋稽核記錄的流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-214">Here's the process for searching the audit log in Office 365.</span></span>

[<span data-ttu-id="078fd-215">步驟 1：執行稽核記錄搜尋</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-215">Step 1: Run an audit log search</span></span>](#step-1-run-an-audit-log-search)

[<span data-ttu-id="078fd-216">步驟 2：檢視搜尋結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-216">Step 2: View the search results</span></span>](#step-2-view-the-search-results)

[<span data-ttu-id="078fd-217">步驟 3：篩選搜尋結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-217">Step 3: Filter the search results</span></span>](#step-3-filter-the-search-results)

[<span data-ttu-id="078fd-218">步驟 4：將搜尋結果匯出至檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-218">Step 4: Export the search results to a file</span></span>](#step-4-export-the-search-results-to-a-file)

### <a name="step-1-run-an-audit-log-search"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-219">步驟 1：執行稽核記錄搜尋</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-219">Step 1: Run an audit log search</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="078fd-220">請移至 [https://protection.office.com](https://protection.office.com)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-220">Go to [https://protection.office.com](https://protection.office.com).</span></span>

    > [!TIP]
    > <span data-ttu-id="078fd-221">您可以使用私密瀏覽工作階段 (而非一般工作階段) 存取安全性與合規性中心，藉此避免您目前用於登入的認證遭到使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-221">Use a private browsing session (not a regular session) to access the Security & Compliance Center because this will prevent the credential that you are currently logged on with from being used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-222">若要在 Internet Explorer 或 Microsoft Edge 開啟 InPrivate 瀏覽器工作階段，請按 CTRL+SHIFT+P。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-222">To open an InPrivate Browsing session in Internet Explorer or Microsoft Edge, just press CTRL+SHIFT+P.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-223">若要在 Google Chrome 中開啟隱私瀏覽工作階段 (稱為無痕式視窗)，請按 CTRL+SHIFT+N。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-223">To open a private browsing session in Google Chrome (called an incognito window), press CTRL+SHIFT+N.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="078fd-224">使用公司或學校帳戶登入 Office 365。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-224">Sign in to Office 365 using your work or school account.</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="078fd-225">在安全性與合規性中心的左窗格中，按一下 [搜尋]\*\*\*\*，然後按一下 [稽核記錄搜尋]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-225">In the left pane of the Security & Compliance Center, click **Search**, and then click **Audit log search**.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="078fd-226">[稽核記錄搜尋]\*\*\*\* 頁面隨即顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-226">The **Audit log search** page is displayed.</span></span>

    ![設定準則，然後按一下 [搜尋] 即可執行報告](../media/8639d09c-2843-44e4-8b4b-9f45974ff7f1.png)

    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="078fd-228">您必須先開啟稽核記錄功能，才能執行稽核記錄搜尋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-228">You have to first turn on audit logging before you can run an audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-229">如果顯示 [開始記錄使用者和系統管理活動]\*\*\*\* 連結，請按一下它以開啟稽核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-229">If the **Start recording user and admin activity** link is displayed, click it to turn on auditing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-230">(如果您沒有看到此連結，表示貴組織已開啟稽核)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-230">If you don't see this link, auditing has already been turned on for your organization.</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="078fd-231">設定下列搜尋準則：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-231">Configure the following search criteria:</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="078fd-232">a.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-232">a.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-233">**活動**：按一下下拉式清單以顯示您可以搜尋的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-233">**Activities**: Click the drop-down list to display the activities that you can search for.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-234">使用者和系統管理員活動會歸類成各種相關活動的群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-234">User and admin activities are organized in to groups of related activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-235">您可以選取特定活動，或者也可以按一下活動群組名稱以選取該群組中的所有活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-235">You can select specific activities or you can click the activity group name to select all activities in the group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-236">您也可以按一下選定的活動以清除選取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-236">You can also click a selected activity to clear the selection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-237">執行搜尋後，只會顯示選定活動的稽核記錄項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-237">After you run the search, only the audit log entries for the selected activities are displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-238">選取 [顯示所有活動的結果]\*\*\*\* 會顯示選定使用者或使用者群組所執行的所有活動結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-238">Selecting **Show results for all activities** displays results for all activities performed by the selected user or group of users.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="078fd-239">Office 365 稽核記錄中會記錄超過 100 個使用者和系統管理員活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-239">Over 100 user and admin activities are logged in the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-240">請按一下本文主題的 [已稽核活動]\*\*\*\* 索引標籤，以查看各個 Office 365 服務中的每項活動描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-240">Click the **Audited activities** tab at the topic of this article to see the descriptions of every activity in each of the different Office 365 services.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="078fd-241">b.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-241">b.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-242">**開始日期**和**結束日期**：根據預設會選取過去七天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-242">**Start date** and **End date**: The last seven days are selected by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-243">選取日期和時間範圍，以顯示該期間內已發生的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-243">Select a date and time range to display the events that occurred within that period.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-244">日期和時間以國際標準時間 (UTC) 格式表示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-244">The date and time are presented in Coordinated Universal Time (UTC) format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-245">您可以指定的最大日期範圍為 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-245">The maximum date range that you can specify is 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-246">如果選定的日期範圍大於 90 天，則會顯示錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-246">An error is displayed if the selected date range is greater than 90 days.</span></span>

    > [!TIP]
    > <span data-ttu-id="078fd-247">如果您使用的是 90 天的最大日期範圍，請為 [開始日期]\*\*\*\* 選取目前的時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-247">If you're using the maximum date range of 90 days, select the current time for the **Start date**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-248">否則，您會收到一則表示開始日期早於結束日期的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-248">Otherwise, you'll receive an error saying that the start date is earlier than the end date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-249">如果您已開啟過去 90 天中的稽核，最大日期範圍不能在開啟稽核的日期之前開始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-249">If you've turned on auditing within the last 90 days, the maximum date range can't start before the date that auditing was turned on.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="078fd-250">c.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-250">c.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-251">**使用者**：在此方塊中按一下，然後選取要顯示搜尋結果的一或多位使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-251">**Users**: Click in this box and then select one or more users to display search results for.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-252">結果清單會顯示您在此方塊中選取的使用者所執行的選定活動之稽核記錄項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-252">The audit log entries for the selected activity performed by the users you select in this box are displayed in the list of results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-253">若要傳回貴組織中所有使用者 (及服務帳戶) 的項目，請將此方塊保留空白。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-253">Leave this box blank to return entries for all users (and service accounts) in your organization.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="078fd-254">d.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-254">d.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-255">**檔案、資料夾或網站**：輸入整個檔案或資料夾名稱的一部分，以搜尋含有特定關鍵字之資料夾的檔案相關活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-255">**File, folder, or site**: Type some or all of a file or folder name to search for activity related to the file of folder that contains the specified keyword.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-256">您也可以指定檔案或資料夾的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-256">You can also specify a URL of a file or folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-257">如果您使用 URL，請確定您輸入了完整的 URL 路徑，或者，如果您只輸入部分 URL，請不要包含任何特殊字元或空格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-257">If you use a URL, be sure the type the full URL path or if you type a portion of the URL, don't include any special characters or spaces.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="078fd-258">若要傳回貴組織中所有檔案和資料夾的項目，請將此方塊保留空白。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-258">Leave this box blank to return entries for all files and folders in your organization.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="078fd-259">**秘訣**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-259">**TIPS**</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="078fd-260">如果您要尋找與**網站**相關的所有活動，在 URL 後面加入萬用字元符號 (\*) 可傳回該網站的所有項目，例如 **"https://contoso-my.sharepoint.com/personal/\*"**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-260">If you're looking for all activities related to a **site**, add the wildcard symbol (\*) after the URL to return all entries for that site; for example, **"https://contoso-my.sharepoint.com/personal/\*"**.</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="078fd-261">如果您要尋找與**檔案**相關的所有活動，在檔案名稱前面加入萬用字元符號 (\*) 可傳回該檔案的所有項目，例如 **"\*Customer_Profitability_Sample.csv"**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-261">If you're looking for all activities related to a **file**, add the wildcard symbol (\*) before the file name to return all entries for that file; for example, **"\*Customer_Profitability_Sample.csv"**.</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="078fd-262">按一下 [搜尋]\*\*\*\* 以使用您的搜尋準則執行搜尋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-262">Click **Search** to run the search using your search criteria.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="078fd-263">搜尋結果隨即載入，而它們在片刻之後會顯示於 [結果]\*\*\*\* 底下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-263">The search results are loaded, and after a few moments they are displayed under **Results**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-264">完成搜尋時，就會顯示找到的結果數量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-264">When the search is finished, the number of results found is displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-265">[結果]\*\*\*\* 窗格中的事件會以 150 個事件為增幅地顯示，上限為 5,000 個事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-265">A maximum of 5,000 events will be displayed in the **Results** pane in increments of 150 events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-266">如果符合搜尋準則的事件超過 5,000 個，則會顯示最新的 5,000 個事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-266">If more than 5,000 events meet the search criteria, the most recent 5,000 events are displayed.</span></span>

   ![搜尋完成後，會顯示結果數目。](../media/986216f1-ca2f-4747-9480-e232b5bf094c.png)

#### <a name="tips-for-searching-the-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-268">搜尋稽核記錄的祕訣</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-268">Tips for searching the audit log</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-269">您可以按一下活動名稱，以選取要搜尋的特定活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-269">You can select specific activities to search for by clicking the activity name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-270">或者您也可以按一下群組名稱，以搜尋群組中的所有活動 (例如 [檔案和資料夾活動]\*\*\*\*)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-270">Or you can search for all activities in a group (such as **File and folder activities**) by clicking the group name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-271">如果已選取活動，您可以按一下它以取消選取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-271">If an activity is selected, you can click it to cancel the selection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-272">您也可以使用搜尋方塊顯示含有您輸入的關鍵字之活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-272">You can also use the search box to display the activities that contain the keyword that you type.</span></span>

  ![按一下活動群組名稱以選取所有活動](../media/3cde97cb-6f35-47c0-8612-ecd9c6ac36a3.png)

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-274">您必須在 [活動]\*\*\*\* 清單中選取 [顯示所有活動的結果]\*\*\*\*，才能顯示來自 Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-274">You have to select **Show results for all activities** in the **Activities** list to display events from the Exchange admin audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-275">來自此稽核記錄的事件會在結果的 [活動]\*\*\*\* 欄中顯示 Cmdlet 名稱 (例如 **Set-Mailbox**)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-275">Events from this audit log display a cmdlet name (for example, **Set-Mailbox**) in the **Activity** column in the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-276">如需詳細資訊，請按一下本主題中的 [已稽核活動]\*\*\*\* 索引標籤，然後按一下 [Exchange 系統管理員活動]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-276">For more information, click the **Audited activities** tab in this topic and then click **Exchange admin activities**.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="078fd-277">同樣地，也會有些稽核活動在 [活動]\*\*\*\* 清單中沒有對應的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-277">Similarly, there are some auditing activities that don't have a corresponding item in the **Activities** list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-278">若您知道這些活動的作業名稱，即可搜尋所有活動，然後在 [活動]\*\*\*\* 欄的方塊中輸入作業名稱來篩選結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-278">If you know the name of the operation for these activities, you can search for all activities, then filter the results by typing the name of the operation in the box for the **Activity** column.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-279">請參閱[步驟 3：篩選搜尋結果](#step-3-filter-the-search-results)，以了解更多有關篩選結果的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-279">See [Step 3: Filter the search results](#step-3-filter-the-search-results) for more information about filtering the results.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-280">按一下 [清除]\*\*\*\* 以清除目前的搜尋準則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-280">Click **Clear** to clear the current search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-281">日期範圍會回到過去七天的預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-281">The date range returns to the default of the last seven days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-282">您也可以按一下 [清除全部以顯示所有活動的結果]\*\*\*\*，以取消所有選定的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-282">You can also click **Clear all to show results for all activities** to cancel all selected activities.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-283">如果找到 5,000 個結果，您可能可以假設有超過 5,000 個符合搜尋準則的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-283">If 5,000 results are found, you can probably assume that there are more than 5,000 events that met the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-284">您可以縮小搜尋準則的範圍，並重新執行搜尋以傳回更少的結果，或者也可以選取 [匯出結果]\*\*\*\* \> [下載所有結果]\*\*\*\*，以匯出所有搜尋結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-284">You can either refine the search criteria and rerun the search to return fewer results, or you can export all of the search results by selecting **Export results** \> **Download all results**.</span></span>

### <a name="step-2-view-the-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-285">步驟 2：檢視搜尋結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-285">Step 2: View the search results</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-286">稽核記錄搜尋的結果會顯示在 [稽核記錄搜尋]\*\*\*\* 頁面的 [結果]\*\*\*\* 底下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-286">The results of an audit log search are displayed under **Results** on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-287">如先前所述，系統最多可顯示 5,000 個 (最新) 事件，每向下捲動一次則可顯示 150 個事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-287">As previously stated a maximum of 5,000 (newest) events are displayed in increments of 150 events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-288">若要顯示更多事件，您可以在 [結果]\*\*\*\* 窗格中使用捲軸列，或按 **Shift + End** 顯示後續 150 個事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-288">To display more events you can use the scroll bar in the **Results** pane or you can press **Shift + End** to display the next 150 events.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-289">結果會包含搜尋所傳回之每個事件的下列相關資訊：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-289">The results contain the following information about each event returned by the search:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-290">**日期：** 事件發生時的日期和時間 (以 UTC 格式顯示)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-290">**Date**: The date and time (in UTC format) when the event occurred.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-291">**IP 位址：** 記錄活動時所使用的裝置之 IP 位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-291">**IP address**: The IP address of the device that was used when the activity was logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-292">IP 位址會以 IPv4 或 IPv6 位址格式顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-292">The IP address is displayed in either an IPv4 or IPv6 address format.</span></span>

   > [!NOTE]
  > <span data-ttu-id="078fd-293">針對某些服務，此欄位中顯示的值可能是代表使用者呼叫服務的受信任應用程式 (例如 Office 網頁版應用程式) 的 IP 位址，而不是執行活動的人員使用之裝置的 IP 位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-293">For some services, the value displayed in this field might be the IP address for a trusted application (for example, Office on the web apps) calling into the service on behalf of a user and not the IP address of the device used by person who performed the activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-294">此外，針對 Azure Active Directory 相關事件的系統管理員活動 (或由系統帳戶執行的活動)，不會記錄 IP 位址，且此欄位中顯示的值為 `null`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-294">Also, for admin activity (or activity performed by a system account) for Azure Active Directory-related events, the IP address isn't logged and the value displayed in this field is `null`.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-295">**使用者**：執行動作並觸發事件的使用者 (或服務帳戶)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-295">**User**: The user (or service account) who performed the action that triggered the event.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-296">**活動**：使用者執行的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-296">**Activity**: The activity performed by the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-297">這個值對應您在 [活動]\*\*\*\* 下拉式清單中選取的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-297">This value corresponds to the activities that you selected in the **Activities** drop down list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-298">若是來自 Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄的事件，此欄中的這個值則是 Exchange Cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-298">For an event from the Exchange admin audit log, the value in this column is an Exchange cmdlet.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-299">**項目**：已建立或修改為對應活動結果的物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-299">**Item**: The object that was created or modified as a result of the corresponding activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-300">例如，已檢視或修改的檔案或已更新的使用者帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-300">For example, the file that was viewed or modified or the user account that was updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-301">並非所有活動在此資料行中都具有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-301">Not all activities have a value in this column.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-302">**詳細資料**：有關活動的其他詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-302">**Detail**: Additional information about an activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-303">同樣地，並非所有活動都會有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-303">Again, not all activities have a value.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-304">按一下 [結果]\*\*\*\* 底下的欄標頭以將結果排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-304">Click a column header under **Results** to sort the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-305">您可以將結果排序為由 A 至 Z 或由 Z 至 A。按一下 [日期]\*\*\*\* 標頭以將結果排序為由最舊至最新或由最新至最舊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-305">You can sort the results from A to Z or Z to A. Click the **Date** header to sort the results from oldest to newest or newest to oldest.</span></span>

#### <a name="view-the-details-for-a-specific-event"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-306">檢視特定事件的詳細資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-306">View the details for a specific event</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-307">您可以按一下搜尋結果清單中的事件記錄，以檢視更多事件相關的詳細資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-307">You can view more details about an event by clicking the event record in the list of search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-308">含有事件記錄中詳細屬性的 [詳細資料]\*\*\*\* 頁面隨即顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-308">A **Details** page is displayed that contains the detailed properties from the event record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-309">顯示的屬性會以發生事件的 Office 365 服務為依據。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-309">The properties that are displayed depend on the Office 365 service in which the event occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-310">若要顯示這些詳細資料，請按一下 [更多資訊]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-310">To display these details, click **More information**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-311">如需說明，請參閱 [Office 365 稽核記錄中的詳細內容](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-311">For descriptions, see [Detailed properties in the Office 365 audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>

![按一下 [更多資訊] 以檢視稽核記錄事件記錄的詳細屬性。](../media/6df582ae-d339-4735-b1a6-80914fb77a08.png)

### <a name="step-3-filter-the-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-313">步驟 3：篩選搜尋結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-313">Step 3: Filter the search results</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-314">除了排序，您也可以篩選稽核記錄搜尋的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-314">In addition to sorting, you can also filter the results of an audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-315">這是一個可協助您快速篩選特定使用者或活動結果的絕佳功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-315">This is a great feature that can help you quickly filter the results for a specific user or activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-316">您一開始可以建立廣泛的搜尋，然後再快速篩選結果以查看特定事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-316">You can initially create a wide search and then quickly filter the results to see specific events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-317">接著，您可以縮小搜尋準則的範圍，然後重新執行搜尋以傳回一組更小、更精簡的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-317">Then you can narrow the search criteria and rerun the search to return a smaller, more concise set of results.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-318">若要篩選結果：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-318">To filter the results:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="078fd-319">執行稽核記錄搜尋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-319">Run an audit log search.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="078fd-320">當顯示結果時，按一下 [篩選結果]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-320">When the results are displayed, click **Filter results**.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="078fd-321">關鍵字方塊隨即顯示在每個欄標頭底下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-321">Keyword boxes are displayed under each column header.</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="078fd-322">按一下欄標頭底下的其中一個方塊，然後輸入字詞或片語 (視您正在篩選的欄而定)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-322">Click one of the boxes under a column header and type a word or phrase, depending on the column you're filtering on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-323">結果將動態重新調整為顯示與您的篩選相符之事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-323">The results will dynamically readjust to display the events that match your filter.</span></span>

   ![在篩選中輸入一個單字以顯示符合篩選的事件](../media/542dc323-a997-402c-934b-cc5e218e50bc.png)

4. <span data-ttu-id="078fd-325">若要清除篩選，請按一下篩選方塊中的 [X]\*\*\*\*，或按一下 [隱藏篩選]\*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-325">To clear a filter, click the **X** in the filter box or click **Hide filtering**.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-326">若要顯示來自 Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄的事件，請在 [活動]\*\*\*\* 篩選方塊中輸入 **-** (破折號)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-326">To display events from the Exchange admin audit log, type a **-** (dash) in the **Activity** filter box.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-327">這會顯示那些顯示於 Exchange 系統管理員事件 [活動]\*\*\*\* 欄中的 Cmdlet 名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-327">This will display cmdlet names, which are displayed in the **Activity** column for Exchange admin events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-328">接著，您可以將 Cmdlet 名稱依字母順序排序顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-328">Then you can sort the cmdlet names in alphabetical order.</span></span>

### <a name="step-4-export-the-search-results-to-a-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-329">步驟 4：將搜尋結果匯出至檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-329">Step 4: Export the search results to a file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-330">您可以將稽核記錄搜尋的結果匯出至您本機電腦上的逗點分隔值 (CSV) 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-330">You can export the results of an audit log search to a comma-separated value (CSV) file on your local computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-331">您可以在 Microsoft Excel 中開啟此檔案，並使用搜尋、排序、篩選，以及將單一欄 (含有多重屬性) 分割為多個欄等功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-331">You can open this file in Microsoft Excel and use features such as search, sorting, filtering, and splitting a single column (that contains multiple properties) into multiple columns.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="078fd-332">執行稽核記錄搜尋，然後修改搜尋準則，直到您獲得想要的結果為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-332">Run an audit log search, and then revise the search criteria until you have the desired results.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="078fd-333">按一下 [匯出結果]\*\*\*\*，然後選取下列其中一個選項：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-333">Click **Export results** and select one of the following options:</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="078fd-334">**儲存載入的結果**：選擇此選項以僅匯出顯示在 [稽核記錄搜尋]\*\*\*\* 頁面 [結果]\*\*\*\* 底下的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-334">**Save loaded results**: Choose this option to export only the entries that are displayed under **Results** on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-335">下載的 CSV 檔案會包含與頁面上顯示相同的欄 (及資料) (日期、使用者、活動、項目及詳細資料)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-335">The CSV file that is downloaded contains the same columns (and data) displayed on the page (Date, User, Activity, Item, and Details).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-336">CSV 檔案中包括一個額外的欄 (命名為 [更多]\*\*\*\*)，其中含有更多來自稽核記錄項目的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-336">An extra column (named **More**) is included in the CSV file that contains more information from the audit log entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-337">因為您正在匯出 [稽核記錄搜尋]\*\*\*\* 頁面上所載入的相同結果 (且可檢視)，因此最多可匯出 5,000 個項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-337">Because you're exporting the same results that are loaded (and viewable) on the **Audit log search** page, a maximum of 5,000 entries are exported.</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="078fd-338">**下載所有結果**：選擇此選項以從符合搜尋準則的 Office 365 稽核記錄匯出所有項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-338">**Download all results**: Choose this option to export all entries from the Office 365 audit log that meet the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-339">針對大量的搜尋結果，選擇此選項除了會下載 [稽核記錄搜尋]\*\*\*\* 頁面上顯示的 5,000 個稽核記錄以外，還會從稽核記錄下載所有項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-339">For a large set of search results, choose this option to download all entries from the audit log in addition to the 5,000 audit records that can be displayed on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-340">此選項會從稽核記錄下載原始資料至 CSV 檔案，並且在一個命名為 **AuditData** 的欄中包含來自稽核記錄項目的其他資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-340">This option downloads the raw data from the audit log to a CSV file, and contains additional information from the audit log entry in a column named **AuditData**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-341">如果您選擇此匯出選項，下載檔案可能需要較久的時間。這是因為如果您選擇其他選項，檔案可能會遠大於下載的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-341">It may take longer to download the file if you choose this export option because the file may be much larger than the one that's downloaded if you choose the other option.</span></span>

     > [!IMPORTANT]
     > <span data-ttu-id="078fd-342">您可以從單一稽核記錄搜尋下載最多 50,000 個項目至 CSV 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-342">You can download a maximum of 50,000 entries to a CSV file from a single audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-343">如果已下載 50,000 個項目至 CSV 檔案，您可能可以假設有超過 50,000 個符合搜尋準則的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-343">If 50,000 entries are downloaded to the CSV file, you can probably assume there are more than 50,000 events that met the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-344">若要匯出的內容超過此限制，請嘗試使用日期範圍來縮小稽核記錄項目的數量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-344">To export more than this limit, try using a date range to reduce the number of audit log entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-345">您可能需要使用較小的日期範圍執行多次搜尋，以匯出 50,000 個以上的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-345">You might have to run multiple searches with smaller date ranges to export more than 50,000 entries.</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="078fd-346">選取匯出選項後，視窗底部就會顯示一則訊息，提示您開啟 CSV 檔案、將它儲存至 [下載] 資料夾，或將它儲存至特定資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-346">After you select an export option, a message is displayed at the bottom of the window that prompts you to open the CSV file, save it to the Downloads folder, or save it to a specific folder.</span></span>

#### <a name="more-information-about-exporting-and-viewing-audit-log-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-347">有關匯出及檢視稽核記錄搜尋結果的更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-347">More information about exporting and viewing audit log search results</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-348">如果您下載所有搜尋結果，CSV 檔案會包含一個命名為 **AuditData** 的欄，其中含有每個事件相關的其他資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-348">If you download all search results, the CSV file contains a column named **AuditData**, which contains additional information about each event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-349">此欄資料包含的 JSON 物件具有稽核記錄中的多個屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-349">The data in this column consists of a JSON object that contains multiple properties from the audit log record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-350">JSON 物件中的每個「屬性：值」\*\* 配對都會以逗號分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-350">Each *property:value* pair in the JSON object is separated by a comma.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-351">您可以在 Excel 的 Power Query 編輯器中使用 JSON 轉換工具，將 **AuditData** 欄分割成多個欄，好讓 JSON 物件中的每個屬性都有自己的欄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-351">You can use the JSON transform tool in the Power Query Editor in Excel to split **AuditData** column into multiple columns so that each property in the JSON object has its own column.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-352">這樣您就可以排序及篩選一或多個屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-352">This lets you sort and filter on one or more of these properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-353">如需使用 Power Query 編輯器轉換 JSON 物件的逐步指示，請參閱[匯出、設定及檢視稽核記錄檔的記錄](export-view-audit-log-records.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-353">For step-by-step instructions using the Power Query Editor to transform the JSON object, see [Export, configure, and view audit log records](export-view-audit-log-records.md).</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="078fd-354">分割 [AuditData]\*\*\*\* 欄後，您可以在 [作業]\*\*\*\* 欄篩選，以顯示特定活動類型的詳細屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-354">After you split the **AuditData** column, you can filter on the **Operations** column to display the detailed properties for a specific type of activity.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-355">[下載所有結果]\*\*\*\* 選項會從 Office 365 稽核記錄下載原始資料至 CSV 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-355">The **Download all results** option downloads the raw data from the Office 365 audit log to a CSV file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-356">如果您選取 [儲存載入的結果]\*\*\*\* 選項，此檔案會包含與下載檔案不同的欄名稱 (CreationDate、UserIds、Operation、AuditData)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-356">This file contains different column names (CreationDate, UserIds, Operation, AuditData) than the file that's downloaded if you select the **Save loaded results** option.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-357">在兩個不同的 CSV 檔案中，相同活動的值可能也會不一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-357">The values in the two different CSV files for the same activity may also be different.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-358">例如，CSV 檔案 [動作]\*\*\*\* 欄中的活動，以及可能會有與 [稽核記錄搜尋]\*\*\*\* 頁面的 [活動]\*\*\*\* 欄中顯示的「使用者易記」名稱不同的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-358">For example, the activity in the **Action** column in the CSV file and may have a different value than the "user-friendly" name that's displayed in the **Activity** column on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-359">例如，「MailboxLogin」與「使用者已登入信箱」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-359">For example, MailboxLogin vs. User signed in to mailbox.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-360">當您從搜尋查詢下載所有結果時，如果搜尋查詢包含不同 Office 365 服務中的事件，則 CSV 檔案中的 [AuditData]\*\*\*\* 欄會包含不同的屬性，視在何種服務中執行動作而定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-360">When you download all results from a search query that contains events from different Office 365 services, the **AuditData** column in the CSV file contains different properties depending on which service the action was performed in.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-361">例如，來自 Exchange 和 Azure AD 稽核記錄的項目包括命名為 **ResultStatus** 的屬性，它會指出執行的動作是否成功。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-361">For example, entries from Exchange and Azure AD audit logs include a property named **ResultStatus** that indicates if the action was successful or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-362">SharePoint 中的事件不包括此屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-362">This property isn't included for events in SharePoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-363">同樣地，SharePoint 事件有一個屬性可用來識別網站 URL 中的檔案和資料夾相關活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-363">Similarly, SharePoint events have a property that identifies the site URL for file and folder-related activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-364">若要減少此行為，請考慮使用不同的搜尋，以匯出來自單一服務的活動結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-364">To mitigate this behavior, consider using different searches to export the results for activities from a single service.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="078fd-365">如需下載所有結果時，CSV 檔案 [AuditData]\*\*\*\* 欄中列出的多個屬性描述，以及各個適用的服務，請參閱 [Office 365 稽核記錄中的詳細屬性](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-365">For a description of many of the properties that are listed in the **AuditData** column in the CSV file when you download all results, and the service each one applies to, see [Detailed properties in the Office 365 audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>

## <a name="audited-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-366">已稽核活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-366">Audited activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-367">本節中各表格說明的是 Office 365 中已稽核的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-367">The tables in this section describe the activities that are audited in Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-368">您可以透過搜尋安全性與合規性中心中的稽核記錄來搜尋這些事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-368">You can search for these events by searching the audit log in the security and compliance center.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-369">這些表格會將相關或來自特定 Office 365 服務的活動集合成一個群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-369">These tables group related activities or the activities from a specific Office 365 service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-370">這些表格包括 [活動]\*\*\*\* 下拉式清單中顯示的易記名稱，以及在稽核記錄詳細資訊中，或匯出搜尋結果時在 CSV 檔案中顯示的對應作業名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-370">The tables include the friendly name that's displayed in the **Activities** drop-down list and the name of the corresponding operation that appears in the detailed information of an audit record and in the CSV file when you export the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-371">如需詳細資訊的說明，請參閱 [Office 365 稽核記錄中的詳細內容](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-371">For descriptions of the detailed information, see [Detailed properties in the Office 365 audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-372">請按一下下列其中一個連結，以移至特定表格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-372">Click one of the following links to go to a specific table.</span></span>

### <a name="file-and-page-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-402">檔案和頁面活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-402">File and page activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-403">下表說明 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 的檔案和頁面活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-403">The following table describes the file and page activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-404">**易記名稱**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-404">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-405">**作業**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-405">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-406">**描述**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-406">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-407">已存取檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-407">Accessed file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-408">FileAccessed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-408">FileAccessed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-409">使用者或系統帳戶存取檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-409">User or system account accesses a file.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-410">(無)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-410">(none)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-411">FileAccessedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-411">FileAccessedExtended</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-412">這與「已存取檔案」(FileAccessed) 活動相關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-412">This is related to the "Accessed file" (FileAccessed) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-413">當相同人員持續存取某個檔案一段時間 (最多 3 小時)，便會記錄 FileAccessedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-413">A FileAccessedExtended event is logged when the same person continually accesses a file for an extended period (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-414">記錄 FileAccessedExtended 事件的目的在於減少持續存取某個檔案時，記錄 FileAccessed 事件的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-414">The purpose of logging FileAccessedExtended events is to reduce the number of FileAccessed events that are logged when a file is continually accessed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-415">這有助於減少多個 FileAccessed 記錄的干擾，以了解哪些基本上是同樣的使用者活動，並讓您專注在初始 (且更重要的) FileAccessed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-415">This helps reduce the noise of multiple FileAccessed records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) FileAccessed event.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-416">已變更合規性原則標籤</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-416">Changed compliance policy label</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-417">ComplianceSettingChanged</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-417">ComplianceSettingChanged</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-418">保留標籤已在文件中套用或移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-418">A retention label was applied to or removed from a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-419">手動或自動將保留標籤套用到郵件時就會觸發此事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-419">This event is triggered when a retention label is manually or automatically applied to a message.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-420">已將記錄狀態變更為鎖定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-420">Changed record status to locked</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-421">LockRecord</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-421">LockRecord</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-422">將文件歸類為記錄的保留標籤記錄狀態已鎖定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-422">The record status of a retention label that classifies a document as a record was locked.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-423">這表示文件無法修改或刪除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-423">This means the document can't be modified or deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-424">只有至少獲派網站參與者權限的使用者可以變更文件記錄狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-424">Only users assigned at least the contributor permission for a site can change the record status of a document.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-454">偵測到的文件敏感度不相符</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-454">Detected document sensitivity mismatch</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-455">DocumentSensitivityMismatchDetected</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-455">DocumentSensitivityMismatchDetected</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-456">使用者將文件上傳到受敏感度標籤保護的網站，且文件的敏感度標籤優先於網站的敏感度標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-456">User uploads a document to a site that's protected with a sensitivity label and the document has a higher priority sensitivity label than the sensitivity label applied to the site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-457">例如，套用「機密」標籤的文件上傳到套用「一般」標籤的網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-457">For example, a document labeled Confidential is uploaded to a site labeled General.</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-458">如果文件套用的敏感度標籤，其優先順序低於網站所套用的敏感度標籤，則不會觸發此事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-458">This event isn't triggered if the document has a lower priority sensitivity label than the sensitivity label applied to the site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-459">例如，套用「一般」標籤的文件上傳到標記為「機密」的網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-459">For example, a document labeled General is uploaded to a site labeled Confidential.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-460">如需敏感度標籤優先順序的詳細資訊，請參閱[標籤優先順序 (順序很重要)](sensitivity-labels.md#label-priority-order-matters)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-460">For more information about sensitivity label priority, see [Label priority (order matters)](sensitivity-labels.md#label-priority-order-matters).</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-474">(無)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-474">(none)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-475">FileModifiedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-475">FileModifiedExtended</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-476">這與「已修改檔案」(FileModified) 活動相關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-476">This is related to the "Modified file" (FileModified) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-477">當相同人員持續修改某個檔案一段時間 (最多 3 小時)，便會記錄 FileModifiedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-477">A FileModifiedExtended event is logged when the same person continually modifies a file for an extended period (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-478">記錄 FileModifiedExtended 事件的目的在於減少持續修改某個檔案時，記錄 FileModified 事件的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-478">The purpose of logging FileModifiedExtended events is to reduce the number of FileModified events that are logged when a file is continually modified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-479">這有助於減少多個 FileModified 記錄的干擾，以了解哪些基本上是同樣的使用者活動，並讓您專注在初始 (且更重要的) FileModified 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-479">This helps reduce the noise of multiple FileModified records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) FileModified event.</span></span>|
