|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-512">已檢視頁面</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-512">Viewed page</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-513">PageViewed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-513">PageViewed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-514">使用者檢視網站上的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-514">User views a page on a site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-515">這不包括使用網頁瀏覽器檢視文件庫中的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-515">This doesn't include using a Web browser to view files located in a document library.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-516">(無)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-516">(none)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-517">PageViewedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-517">PageViewedExtended</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-518">這與「已檢視頁面」(PageViewed) 活動相關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-518">This is related to the "Viewed page" (PageViewed) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-519">當相同人員持續檢視某個網頁一段時間 (最多 3 小時)，便會記錄 PageViewedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-519">A PageViewedExtended event is logged when the same person continually views a web page for an extended period (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-520">記錄 PageViewedExtended 事件的目的在於減少持續檢視某個頁面時，記錄 PageViewed 事件的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-520">The purpose of logging PageViewedExtended events is to reduce the number of PageViewed events that are logged when a page is continually viewed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-521">這有助於減少多個 PageViewed 記錄的干擾，以了解哪些基本上是同樣的使用者活動，並讓您專注在初始 (且更重要的) PageViewed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-521">This helps reduce the noise of multiple PageViewed records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) PageViewed event.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-522">用戶端發出的檢視訊號</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-522">View signaled by client</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-523">ClientViewSignaled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-523">ClientViewSignaled</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-524">使用者的用戶端 (例如網站或行動應用程式) 已發出訊號，指出使用者已檢視指示的頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-524">A user's client (such as website or mobile app) has signaled that the indicated page has been viewed by the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-525">此活動通常會在頁面的 PagePrefetched 事件之後進行記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-525">This activity is often logged following a PagePrefetched event for a page.</span></span> <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="078fd-526">**請注意**：由於 ClientViewSignaled 事件會由用戶端發出訊號，而不是由伺服器，所以伺服器可能不會記錄事件，因此事件可能也不會出現在稽核記錄中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-526">**NOTE**: Because ClientViewSignaled events are signaled by the client, rather than the server, it's possible the event may not be logged by the server and therefore may not appear in the audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-527">稽核記錄中的資訊也可能不可靠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-527">It's also possible that information in the audit record may not be trustworthy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-528">不過，因為用來建立訊號的權杖會驗證使用者的身分識別，因此對應稽核記錄中所列的使用者身分識別會是正確的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-528">However, because the user's identity is validated by the token used to create the signal, the user's identity listed in the corresponding audit record is accurate.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-529">(無)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-529">(none)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-530">PagePrefetched</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-530">PagePrefetched</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-531">使用者的用戶端 (例如網站或行動應用程式) 已要求指示的頁面在使用者瀏覽至此時，協助改善效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-531">A user's client (such as website or mobile app) has requested the indicated page to help improve performance if the user browses to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-532">記錄此事件的目的是指出頁面內容已對使用者的用戶端提供服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-532">This event is logged to indicate that the page content has been served to the user's client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-533">此事件並非明確指示使用者已瀏覽到此頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-533">This event isn't a definitive indication that the user navigated to the page.</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-534">當用戶端呈現頁面內容時 (根據使用者的要求)，應該會隨即產生 ClientViewSignaled 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-534">When the page content is rendered by the client (as per the user's request) a ClientViewSignaled event should be generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-535">並非所有用戶端都支援指出預先擷取活動，因此某些預先擷取的活動可能會記錄為 PageViewed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-535">Not all clients support indicating a pre-fetch, and therefore some pre-fetched activities might instead be logged as PageViewed events.</span></span>|
||||

#### <a name="the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-536">稽核記錄中的 app\@sharepoint 使用者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-536">The app\@sharepoint user in audit records</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-537">在部分檔案活動 (以及其他 SharePoint 相關活動) 的稽核記錄中，您可能會注意到執行活動的使用者 ([User] 和 [UserId] 欄位中識別) 為 app@sharepoint。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-537">In audit records for some file activities (and other SharePoint-related activities), you may notice the user who performed the activity (identified in the User and UserId fields) is app@sharepoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-538">這表示執行活動的「使用者」是應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-538">This indicates that the "user" who performed the activity was an application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-539">在此情況下，應用程式會獲授與 SharePoint 中的權限，以代表使用者、系統管理員或服務執行整個組織的動作 (例如搜尋 SharePoint 網站或 OneDrive 帳戶)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-539">In this case, the application was granted permissions in SharePoint to perform organization-wide actions (such as search a SharePoint site or OneDrive account) on behalf of a user, admin, or service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-540">這種將權限授與應用程式的程序稱為*僅限 SharePoint 應用程式*存取權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-540">This process of giving permissions to an application is called *SharePoint App-Only* access.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-541">這表示向 SharePoint 呈現，可執行動作的驗證是由應用程式 (而不是使用者) 所建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-541">This indicates that the authentication presented to SharePoint to perform an action was made by an application, instead of a user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-542">這就是在特定稽核記錄中識別 app@sharepoint 使用者的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-542">This is why the app@sharepoint user is identified in certain audit records.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-543">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[授與使用僅限 SharePoint 應用程式的存取權](https://docs.microsoft.com/sharepoint/dev/solution-guidance/security-apponly-azureacs) \(英文\)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-543">For more information, see [Grant access using SharePoint App-Only](https://docs.microsoft.com/sharepoint/dev/solution-guidance/security-apponly-azureacs).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-544">例如，app@sharepoint 通常會標示為「執行搜尋查詢」和「存取檔案」事件的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-544">For example, app@sharepoint is often identified as the user for "Performed search query" and "Accessed file" events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-545">這是因為當您將保留原則套用至網站和 OneDrive 帳戶時，組織中擁有僅限 SharePoint 應用程式存取權的應用程式會執行搜尋查詢和存取檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-545">That's because an application with SharePoint App-Only access in your organization performs search queries and accesses files when applying retention policies to sites and OneDrive accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-546">以下是一些其他案例，其中 app@sharepoint 在稽核記錄中可能會識別為執行活動的使用者：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-546">Here are a few other scenarios where app@sharepoint may be identified in an audit record as the user who performed an activity:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-547">Office 365 群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-547">Office 365 Groups.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-548">當使用者或系統管理員建立新群組時，系統會產生稽核記錄，以建立網站集合、更新清單，以及將成員新增至 SharePoint 群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-548">When a user or admin creates a new group, audit records are generated for creating a site collection, updating lists, and adding members to a SharePoint group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-549">這些工作是應用程式代表建立群組的使用者執行的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-549">These tasks are performed an application on behalf of the user who created the group.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-550">Microsoft Teams。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-550">Microsoft Teams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-551">與 Office 365 群組類似，建立新小組時，系統會產生稽核記錄，以建立網站集合、更新清單，以及將成員新增至 SharePoint 群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-551">Similar to Office 365 groups, audit records are generated for creating a site collection, updating lists, and adding members to a SharePoint group when a team is created.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-552">合規性功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-552">Compliance features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-553">當系統管理員實作合規性功能時，例如保留原則、電子文件探索保留及自動套用靈敏度標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-553">When an admin implements compliance features, such as retention policies, eDiscovery holds, and auto-applying sensitivity labels.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-554">在這些及其他案例中，您也會注意到以 app@sharepoint 作為指定之使用者的稽核記錄是在非常短的時間內建立的，彼此之間的間隔通常為幾秒鐘。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-554">In these and other scenarios, you'll also notice that multiple audit records with app@sharepoint as the specified user were created within a very short time frame, often within a few seconds of each other.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-555">這也表示這些稽核記錄可能是由相同使用者啟動的工作所觸發。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-555">This also indicates they were probably triggered by the same user-initiated task.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-556">此外，稽核記錄中的 [ApplicationDisplayName] 和 [EventData] 欄位可協助您識別觸發此事件的案例或應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-556">Also, the ApplicationDisplayName and EventData fields in the audit record may help you identify the scenario or application that triggered the event.</span></span>

### <a name="folder-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-557">資料夾活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-557">Folder activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-558">下表說明 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 的資料夾活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-558">The following table describes the folder activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-559">如先前所述，某些 SharePoint 活動的稽核記錄將會指出 app@sharepoint 使用者代表啟動動作的使用者或系統管理員執行了動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-559">As previously explained, audit records for some SharePoint activities will indicate the app@sharepoint user performed the activity of behalf of the user or admin who initiated the action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-560">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[稽核記錄中的 app\@sharepoint 使用者](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-560">For more information, see [The app\@sharepoint user in audit records](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-561">**易記名稱**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-561">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-562">**作業**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-562">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-563">**描述**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-563">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-564">已複製資料夾</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-564">Copied folder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-565">FolderCopied</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-565">FolderCopied</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-566">使用者從網站複製資料夾至 SharePoint 或商務用 OneDrive 中的另一個位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-566">User copies a folder from a site to another location in SharePoint or OneDrive for Business.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-567">已建立資料夾</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-567">Created folder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-568">FolderCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-568">FolderCreated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-569">使用者在網站上建立資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-569">User creates a folder on a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-570">已刪除資料夾</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-570">Deleted folder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-571">FolderDeleted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-571">FolderDeleted</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-572">使用者刪除網站上的資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-572">User deletes a folder from a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-573">已刪除資源回收筒中的資料夾</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-573">Deleted folder from recycle bin</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-574">FolderDeletedFirstStageRecycleBin</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-574">FolderDeletedFirstStageRecycleBin</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-575">使用者從網站的資源回收筒中刪除資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-575">User deletes a folder from the recycle bin on a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-576">已刪除第二階段資源回收筒中的資料夾</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-576">Deleted folder from second-stage recycle bin</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-577">FolderDeletedSecondStageRecycleBin</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-577">FolderDeletedSecondStageRecycleBin</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-578">使用者從網站的第二階段資源回收筒中刪除資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-578">User deletes a folder from the second-stage recycle bin on a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-579">已修改資料夾</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-579">Modified folder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-580">FolderModified</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-580">FolderModified</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-581">使用者修改網站上的資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-581">User modifies a folder on a site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-582">這包括變更資料夾的中繼資料，例如變更標籤和屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-582">This includes changing the folder metadata, such as changing tags and properties.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-583">已移動資料夾</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-583">Moved folder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-584">FolderMoved</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-584">FolderMoved</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-585">使用者將資料夾移動至網站上的其他位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-585">User moves a folder to a different location on a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-586">已重新命名資料夾</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-586">Renamed folder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-587">FolderRenamed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-587">FolderRenamed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-588">使用者在網站上重新命名資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-588">User renames a folder on a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-589">已還原資料夾</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-589">Restored folder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-590">FolderRestored</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-590">FolderRestored</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-591">使用者從網站的資源回收筒中還原已刪除的資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-591">User restores a deleted folder from the recycle bin on a site.</span></span>|

### <a name="sharepoint-list-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-592">SharePoint 清單活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-592">SharePoint list activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-593">下表說明使用者在 SharePoint Online 中與清單和清單項目互動時的相關活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-593">The following table describes activities related to when users interact with lists and list items in SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-594">如先前所述，某些 SharePoint 活動的稽核記錄將會指出 app@sharepoint 使用者代表啟動動作的使用者或系統管理員執行了動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-594">As previously explained, audit records for some SharePoint activities will indicate the app@sharepoint user performed the activity of behalf of the user or admin who initiated the action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-595">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[稽核記錄中的 app\@sharepoint 使用者](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-595">For more information, see [The app\@sharepoint user in audit records](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-596">**易記名稱**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-596">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-597">**作業**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-597">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-598">**描述**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-598">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-599">已建立清單</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-599">Created list</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-600">ListCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-600">ListCreated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-601">使用者已建立 SharePoint 清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-601">A user created a SharePoint list.</span></span>|

### <a name="sharing-and-access-request-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-667">共用及存取要求活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-667">Sharing and access request activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-668">下表說明 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中的使用者共用和存取要求活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-668">The following table describes the user sharing and access request activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-669">針對共用事件，[結果]\*\*\*\* 底下的 [詳細資料]\*\*\*\* 欄會識別共用項目的使用者或群組名稱，以及使用者或群組是否為您的組織中的成員或來賓。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-669">For sharing events, the **Detail** column under **Results** identifies the name of the user or group the item was shared with and whether that user or group is a member or guest in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-670">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[在 Office 365 稽核記錄中使用共用稽核](use-sharing-auditing.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-670">For more information, see [Use sharing auditing in the Office 365 audit log](use-sharing-auditing.md).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-671">根據使用者物件的 UserType 屬性，使用者可以是成員\*\* 或來賓\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-671">Users can be either  *members*  or  *guests*  based on the UserType property of the user object.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-672">成員通常是員工，而來賓通常是您的組織之外的共同作業者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-672">A member is usually an employee, and a guest is usually a collaborator outside of your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-673">當使用者接受共用邀請時 (而且不屬於您的組織的一部分)，就會在您的組織目錄中為他們建立使用者帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-673">When a user accepts a sharing invitation (and isn't already part of your organization), a guest account is created for them in your organization's directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-674">一旦來賓使用者在您的目錄中擁有帳戶後，就可以直接與他們共用資源 (而不需要邀請)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-674">Once the guest user has an account in your directory, resources may be shared directly with them (without requiring an invitation).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-675">**易記名稱**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-675">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-676">**作業**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-676">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-677">**描述**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-677">**Description**</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-678">已將權限等級新增至網站集合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-678">Added permission level to site collection</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-679">PermissionLevelAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-679">PermissionLevelAdded</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-680">權限等級已新增至網站集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-680">A permission level was added to a site collection.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-681">已接受存取要求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-681">Accepted access request</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-682">AccessRequestAccepted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-682">AccessRequestAccepted</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-683">已接受網站、資料夾或文件的存取要求，而提出要求的使用者已獲授與存取權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-683">An access request to a site, folder, or document was accepted and the requesting user has been granted access.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-684">已接受共用邀請</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-684">Accepted sharing invitation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-685">SharingInvitationAccepted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-685">SharingInvitationAccepted</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-686">使用者 (成員或來賓) 已接受共用邀請，並獲授與資源的存取權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-686">User (member or guest) accepted a sharing invitation and was granted access to a resource.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-687">此事件包括受邀的使用者，以及用來接受邀請的電子郵件地址 (它們可能不同) 之相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-687">This event includes information about the user who was invited and the email address that was used to accept the invitation (they could be different).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-688">此活動通常伴隨第二個事件，描述使用者如何獲授與資源的存取權。例如，將使用者新增至擁有資源存取權的群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-688">This activity is often accompanied by a second event that describes how the user was granted access to the resource, for example, adding the user to a group that has access to the resource.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-689">已封鎖的共用邀請</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-689">Blocked sharing invitation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-690">SharingInvitationBlocked</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-690">SharingInvitationBlocked</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-691">貴組織使用者所傳送的共用邀請遭到封鎖，因為外部共用原則會根據目標使用者的網域允許或拒絕外部共用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-691">A sharing invitation sent by a user in your organization is blocked because of an external sharing policy that either allows or denies external sharing based on the domain of the target user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-692">在此案例中，共用邀請因下列原因而遭到刪除：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-692">In this case, the sharing invitation was blocked because:</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-693">允許的網域清單中不包含目標使用者的網域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-693">The target user's domain isn't included in the list of allowed domains.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-694">或者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-694">Or</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-695">封鎖的網域清單中包含目標使用者的網域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-695">The target user's domain is included in the list of blocked domains.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-696">如需根據網域允許或封鎖外部共用的詳細資訊，請參閱[在 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中限制網域共用](https://support.office.com/article/5d7589cd-0997-4a00-a2ba-2320ec49c4e9)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-696">For more information about allowing or blocking external sharing based on domains, see [Restricted domains sharing in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business](https://support.office.com/article/5d7589cd-0997-4a00-a2ba-2320ec49c4e9).</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-697">已建立存取要求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-697">Created access request</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-698">AccessRequestCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-698">AccessRequestCreated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-699">使用者要求他們未擁有存取權限的網站、資料夾或文件之存取權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-699">User requests access to a site, folder, or document they don't have permissions to access.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-700">已建立公司可共用連結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-700">Created a company shareable link</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-701">CompanyLinkCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-701">CompanyLinkCreated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-702">使用者已建立資源的全公司連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-702">User created a company-wide link to a resource.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-703">全公司連結只能讓您組織中的成員使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-703">company-wide links can only be used by members in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-704">來賓無法使用這些連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-704">They can't be used by guests.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-705">已建立匿名連結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-705">Created an anonymous link</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-706">AnonymousLinkCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-706">AnonymousLinkCreated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-707">使用者已建立資源的匿名連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-707">User created an anonymous link to a resource.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-708">任何人只要有此連結就可以存取資源，而不需要驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-708">Anyone with this link can access the resource without having to be authenticated.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-709">已建立安全連結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-709">Created secure link</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-710">SecureLinkCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-710">SecureLinkCreated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-711">已對此項目建立安全共用連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-711">A secure sharing link was created to this item.</span></span>|

### <a name="synchronization-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-767">同步處理活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-767">Synchronization activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-768">下表列出 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中的檔案同步活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-768">The following table lists file synchronization activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-769">**易記名稱**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-769">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-770">**作業**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-770">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-771">**描述**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-771">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-772">已允許電腦同步處理檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-772">Allowed computer to sync files</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-773">ManagedSyncClientAllowed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-773">ManagedSyncClientAllowed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-774">使用者與網站成功建立同步處理關聯性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-774">User successfully establishes a sync relationship with a site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-775">同步關係成功，因為使用者的電腦是已新增至網域清單之網域的成員 (稱為「安全收件者清單」\*\*)，可以存取您的組織中的文件庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-775">The sync relationship is successful because the user's computer is a member of a domain that's been added to the list of domains (called the *safe recipients list*) that can access document libraries in your organization.</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-776">如需有關此功能的詳細資訊，請參閱[使用 Windows PowerShell Cmdlet 為安全收件者清單上的網域啟用 OneDrive 同步](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-776">For more information about this feature, see [Use Windows PowerShell cmdlets to enable OneDrive sync for domains that are on the safe recipients list](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609).</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-777">已阻擋電腦同步處理檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-777">Blocked computer from syncing files</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-778">UnmanagedSyncClientBlocked</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-778">UnmanagedSyncClientBlocked</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-779">使用者嘗試與網站建立同步關聯性，但作為連線來源的電腦並非您組織網域的成員或是未加入網域清單 (也稱為安全收件者清單)\*\* 中的網域成員，加入此清單者才可存取您組織中的文件庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-779">User tries to establish a sync relationship with a site from a computer that isn't a member of your organization's domain or is a member of a domain that hasn't been added to the list of domains (called the  *safe recipients list)*  that can access document libraries in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-780">不允許同步關係，並且禁止使用者的電腦同步、下載或上傳文件庫的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-780">The sync relationship is not allowed, and the user's computer is blocked from syncing, downloading, or uploading files on a document library.</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-781">如需此功能的相關資訊，請參閱[使用 Windows PowerShell Cmdlet 為安全收件者清單上的網域啟用 OneDrive 同步](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-781">For information about this feature, see [Use Windows PowerShell cmdlets to enable OneDrive sync for domains that are on the safe recipients list](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609).</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-782">已下載檔案至電腦</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-782">Downloaded files to computer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-783">FileSyncDownloadedFull</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-783">FileSyncDownloadedFull</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-784">使用者建立同步處理關聯性，且初次從文件庫成功下載檔案至電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-784">User establishes a sync relationship and successfully downloads files for the first time to their computer from a document library.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-785">已下載檔案變更至電腦</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-785">Downloaded file changes to computer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-786">FileSyncDownloadedPartial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-786">FileSyncDownloadedPartial</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-787">使用者從文件庫成功下載任何檔案變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-787">User successfully downloads any changes to files from a document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-788">此活動表示，對文件庫中檔案所做的任何變更都已下載至使用者的電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-788">This activity indicates that any changes that were made to files in the document library were downloaded to the user's computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-789">因為使用者之前已下載文件庫，所以只會下載變更 (如 [已下載檔案至電腦]\*\* \*\* 活動所指出)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-789">Only changes were downloaded because the document library was previously downloaded by the user (as indicated by the **Downloaded files to computer** activity).</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-790">已下載檔案至文件庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-790">Uploaded files to document library</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-791">FileSyncUploadedFull</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-791">FileSyncUploadedFull</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-792">使用者建立同步處理關聯性，且初次從電腦成功上傳檔案至文件庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-792">User establishes a sync relationship and successfully uploads files for the first time from their computer to a document library.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-793">已上傳檔案變更至文件庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-793">Uploaded file changes to document library</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-794">FileSyncUploadedPartial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-794">FileSyncUploadedPartial</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-795">使用者成功上傳變更至文件庫中的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-795">User successfully uploads changes to files on a document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-796">此事件表示，對來自文件庫的本機版本檔案所做的任何變更已成功上傳至文件庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-796">This event indicates that any changes made to the local version of a file from a document library are successfully uploaded to the document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-797">因為使用者之前已上傳這些檔案 (如 [已上傳檔案至文件庫]\*\*\*\* 活動所指出)，所以只會上傳變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-797">Only changes are uploaded because those files were previously uploaded by the user (as indicated by the **Uploaded files to document library** activity).</span></span>|
||||

### <a name="site-permissions-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-798">網站權限活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-798">Site permissions activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-799">下表列出在 SharePoint 中指派權限及使用群組提供 (及撤銷) 網站存取權的相關事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-799">The following table lists events related to assigning permissions in SharePoint and using groups to give (and revoke) access to sites.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-800">如先前所述，某些 SharePoint 活動的稽核記錄將會指出 app@sharepoint 使用者代表啟動動作的使用者或系統管理員執行了動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-800">As previously explained, audit records for some SharePoint activities will indicate the app@sharepoint user performed the activity of behalf of the user or admin who initiated the action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-801">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[稽核記錄中的 app\@sharepoint 使用者](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-801">For more information, see [The app\@sharepoint user in audit records](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-802">**易記名稱**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-802">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-803">**作業**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-803">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-804">**描述**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-804">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|

### <a name="site-administration-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-866">網站管理活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-866">Site administration activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-867">下表列出 SharePoint Online 中的網站管理工作所產生的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-867">The following table lists events that result from site administration tasks in SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-868">如先前所述，某些 SharePoint 活動的稽核記錄將會指出 app@sharepoint 使用者代表啟動動作的使用者或系統管理員執行了動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-868">As previously explained, audit records for some SharePoint activities will indicate the app@sharepoint user performed the activity of behalf of the user or admin who initiated the action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-869">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[稽核記錄中的 app\@sharepoint 使用者](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-869">For more information, see [The app\@sharepoint user in audit records](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records).</span></span>

### <a name="exchange-mailbox-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-987">Exchange 信箱活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-987">Exchange mailbox activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-988">下表列出信箱稽核記錄可以記錄的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-988">The following table lists the activities that can be logged by mailbox audit logging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-989">信箱擁有者、指定使用者或管理員所執行的信箱活動會記錄在 Office 365 稽核記錄中達 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-989">Mailbox activities performed by the mailbox owner, a delegated user, or an administrator are automatically logged in the Office 365 audit log for up to 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-990">系統管理員可能會關閉組織中所有使用者的信箱稽核記錄功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-990">It's possible for an admin to turn off mailbox audit logging for all users in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-991">在此情況下，任何使用者的信箱動作都不會記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-991">In this case, no mailbox actions for any user are logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-992">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[管理信箱稽核](enable-mailbox-auditing.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-992">For more information, see [Manage mailbox auditing](enable-mailbox-auditing.md).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="078fd-993">您也可以在 Exchange Online PowerShell 中使用 [Search-MailboxAuditLog](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/policy-and-compliance-audit/search-mailboxauditlog) Cmdlet 來搜尋信箱活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-993">You can also search for mailbox activities by using the [Search-MailboxAuditLog](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/policy-and-compliance-audit/search-mailboxauditlog) cmdlet in Exchange Online PowerShell.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-994">**易記名稱**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-994">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-995">**作業**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-995">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-996">**描述**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-996">**Description**</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-997">存取信箱項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-997">Accessed mailbox items</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-998">MailItemsAccessed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-998">MailItemsAccessed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-999">在信箱中讀取或存取郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-999">Messages were read or accessed in mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1000">可以通過以下兩種方式之一觸發此事件的稽核記錄：當郵件客戶端 (例如 Outlook) 對郵件執行繫結作業時，或者當郵件通訊協定 (例如 Exchange ActiveSync 或 IMAP) 同步郵件文件夾中的項目時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1000">Audit records for this activity are triggered in one of two ways: when a mail client (such as Outlook) performs a bind operation on messages or when mail protocols (such as Exchange ActiveSync or IMAP) sync items in a mail folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1001">僅有 Office 365 或 Microsoft 365 E5 授權的使用者可記錄此事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1001">This activity is only logged for users with an Office 365 or Microsoft 365 E5 license.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1002">在調查遭入侵的電子郵件帳戶時，分析此活動的稽核記錄相當實用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1002">Analyzing audit records for this activity is useful when investigating compromised email account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1003">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[進階稽核](advanced-audit.md#access-to-crucial-events-for-investigations)中的〈存取調查重要事件〉一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1003">For more information, see the "Access to crucial events for investigations" section in [Advanced Audit](advanced-audit.md#access-to-crucial-events-for-investigations).</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1004">已新增代理人信箱權限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1004">Added delegate mailbox permissions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1005">AddMailboxPermissions</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1005">AddMailboxPermissions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1006">系統管理員已將另一名人員其信箱的 FullAccess 信箱權限指派給某個使用者 (亦稱為「代理人」)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1006">An administrator assigned the FullAccess mailbox permission to a user (known as a delegate) to another person's mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1007">FullAccess 權限可讓代理人開啟該名人員的信箱，以及讀取和管理信箱的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1007">The FullAccess permission allows the delegate to open the other person's mailbox, and read and manage the contents of the mailbox.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1008">新增或移除具有行事曆資料夾代理人存取權的使用者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1008">Added or removed user with delegate access to calendar folder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1009">UpdateCalendarDelegation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1009">UpdateCalendarDelegation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1010">已新增或移除作為另一個使用者信箱行事曆代理人的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1010">A user was added or removed as a delegate to the calendar of another user's mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1011">行事曆代理可讓其他有相同組織權限的人來管理信箱擁有者的行事曆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1011">Calendar delegation gives someone else in the same organization permissions to manage the mailbox owner's calendar.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1016">已複製郵件到另一個資料夾</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1016">Copied messages to another folder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1017">Copy</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1017">Copy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1018">郵件已複製到另一個資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1018">A message was copied to another folder.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1053">已移除代理人信箱權限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1053">Removed delegate mailbox permissions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1054">Remove-MailboxPermission</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1054">Remove-MailboxPermission</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1055">系統管理員已將 FullAccess 權限 (先前已指派給代理人) 從人員的信箱移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1055">An administrator removed the FullAccess permission (that was assigned to a delegate) from a person's mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1056">移除 FullAccess 權限後，代理人即無法開啟該名人員的信箱或存取其中的任何內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1056">After the FullAccess permission is removed, the delegate can't open the other person's mailbox or access any content in it.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1061">已使用 [傳送為] 權限傳送郵件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1061">Sent message using Send As permissions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1062">SendAs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1062">SendAs</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1063">已使用 [傳送為] 權限傳送郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1063">A message was sent using the SendAs permission.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1064">這表示，另一個使用者已傳送郵件，就像此郵件是來自信箱擁有者一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1064">This means that another user sent the message as though it came from the mailbox owner.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1065">已使用 [代理傳送者] 權限傳送郵件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1065">Sent message using Send On Behalf permissions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1066">SendOnBehalf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1066">SendOnBehalf</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1067">已使用 [代理傳送者] 權限傳送郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1067">A message was sent using the SendOnBehalf permission.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1068">這表示，另一個使用者已代表信箱擁有者傳送郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1068">This means that another user sent the message on behalf of the mailbox owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1069">此郵件會向收件者指出誰代理傳送郵件，以及實際上是誰傳送郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1069">The message indicates to the recipient who the message was sent on behalf of and who actually sent the message.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1073">已更新郵件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1073">Updated message</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1074">Update</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1074">Update</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1075">郵件或其屬性已變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1075">A message or its properties was changed.</span></span>|

### <a name="sway-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-1079">Sway 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1079">Sway activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1080">下表列出在 Sway 中的使用者和系統管理員活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1080">The following table lists user and admin activities in Sway.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1081">Sway 是一個 Office 365 App，可協助使用者在互動式 Web 畫布上收集、格式化，以及分享想法、故事及簡報。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1081">Sway is an Office 365 app that helps users gather, format, and share ideas, stories, and presentations on an interactive, web-based canvas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1082">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[關於 Sway 的常見問題集 – 系統管理員說明](https://support.office.com/article/446380fa-25bf-47b2-996c-e12cb2f9d075)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1082">For more information, see [Frequently asked questions about Sway - Admin Help](https://support.office.com/article/446380fa-25bf-47b2-996c-e12cb2f9d075).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1083">**易記名稱**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1083">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1084">**作業**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1084">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1085">**描述**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1085">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|

### <a name="application-administration-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-1188">應用程式管理活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1188">Application administration activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1189">下表列出當管理員新增或變更已在 Azure AD 中註冊的應用程式時，會記錄的應用程式系統管理活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1189">The following table lists application admin activities that are logged when an admin adds or changes an application that's registered in Azure AD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1190">任何依靠 Azure AD 進行驗證的應用程式都必須在目錄中註冊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1190">Any application that relies on Azure AD for authentication must be registered in the directory.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1191">**易記名稱**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1191">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1192">**作業**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1192">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1193">**描述**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1193">**Description**</span></span>|

### <a name="ediscovery-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-1276">電子文件探索活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1276">eDiscovery activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1277">在安全性與合規性中心中或透過執行對應 PowerShell Cmdlet 所進行的內容搜尋和電子文件探索相關活動，會記錄在稽核記錄中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1277">Content Search and eDiscovery-related activities that are performed in the security and compliance center or by running the corresponding PowerShell cmdlets are logged in the audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1278">這包括下列活動：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1278">This includes the following activities:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1279">建立及管理電子文件探索案件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1279">Creating and managing eDiscovery cases</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1280">建立、開啟及編輯 [內容搜尋]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1280">Creating, starting, and editing Content Searches</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1281">執行 [內容搜尋] 動作，例如預覽、匯出及刪除搜尋結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1281">Performing Content Search actions, such as previewing, exporting, and deleting search results</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1282">設定 [內容搜尋] 的權限篩選</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1282">Configuring permissions filtering for Content Search</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1283">管理電子文件探索系統管理員角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1283">Managing the eDiscovery Administrator role</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1284">如需已記錄的電子文件探索活動之清單和詳細描述，請參閱[搜尋 Office 365 稽核記錄中的電子文件探索活動](search-for-ediscovery-activities-in-the-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1284">For a list and detailed description of the eDiscovery activities that are logged, see [Search for eDiscovery activities in the Office 365 audit log](search-for-ediscovery-activities-in-the-audit-log.md).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1285">[活動]\*\*\*\* 下拉式清單中的 [電子文件探索活動]\*\*\*\* 下方所列活動的結果事件，最久需要 30 分鐘才會顯示在搜尋結果中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1285">It takes up to 30 minutes for events that result from the activities listed under **eDiscovery activities** in the **Activities** drop-down list to be displayed in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1286">相反地，系統需要 24 小時才能在搜尋結果中顯示電子文件探索 Cmdlet 活動的對應事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1286">Conversely, it takes up to 24 hours for the corresponding events from eDiscovery cmdlet activities to appear in the search results.</span></span>

### <a name="power-bi-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-1367">Power BI 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1367">Power BI activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1368">您可以在 Power BI 中搜尋活動的稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1368">You can search the audit log for activities in Power BI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1369">如需 Power BI 活動的相關資訊，請參閱[在您組織內使用稽核功能](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-auditing#activities-audited-by-power-bi)中的＜由 Power BI 進行稽核的活動＞一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1369">For information about Power BI activities, see the "Activities audited by Power BI" section in [Using auditing within your organization](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-auditing#activities-audited-by-power-bi).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1370">Power BI 的稽核記錄未預設為啟用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1370">Audit logging for Power BI isn't enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1371">若要在 Office 365 稽核記錄中搜尋 Power BI 活動，您必須在 Power BI 系統管理入口網站中啟用稽核功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1371">To search for Power BI activities in the Office 365 audit log, you have to enable auditing in the Power BI admin portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1372">如需相關指示，請參閱 [Power BI 系統管理員入口網站](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs)中的＜稽核記錄＞一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1372">For instructions, see the "Audit logs" section in [Power BI admin portal](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs).</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-workplace-analytics-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-1373">Microsoft 工作場所分析活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1373">Microsoft Workplace Analytics activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1374">工作場所分析可針對群組在 Office 365 組織間共同作業的方式提供見解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1374">Workplace Analytics provides insight into how groups collaborate across your Office 365 organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1375">下表列出在工作場所分析中獲派系統管理員角色或分析師角色的使用者所執行的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1375">The following table lists activities performed by users that are assigned the Administrator role or the Analyst roles in Workplace Analytics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1376">獲派分析師角色的使用者具有所有服務功能的完整存取權，並可使用產品來進行分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1376">Users assigned the Analyst role have full access to all service features and use the product to do analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1377">獲派系統管理員角色的使用者可以設定隱私權設定與系統預設值，並可以準備、上傳及驗證工作場所分析中的組織資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1377">Users assigned the Administrator role can configure privacy settings and system defaults, and can prepare, upload, and verify organizational data in Workplace Analytics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1378">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[工作場所分析](https://docs.microsoft.com/workplace-analytics/index-orig)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1378">For more information, see [Workplace Analytics](https://docs.microsoft.com/workplace-analytics/index-orig).</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-teams-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-1412">Microsoft Teams 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1412">Microsoft Teams activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1413">下表列出 Office 365 稽核記錄中記錄的 Microsoft Teams 使用者和系統管理員活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1413">The following table lists the user and admin activities in Microsoft Teams that are logged in the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1414">Microsoft Teams 是 Office 365 中以聊天方式為主的工作區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1414">Microsoft Teams is a chat-centered workspace in Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1415">它能將小組的交談、會議、檔案及筆記存放在同一個位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1415">It brings a team's conversations, meetings, files, and notes together into a single place.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1416">如需詳細資訊以及說明主題的連結，請參閱：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1416">For more information and links to help topics, see:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1417">Microsoft Teams 的常見問題集 - 系統管理員說明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1417">Frequently asked questions about Microsoft Teams - Admin Help</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/05cbe533-2181-4e95-a4b0-52cd7695fafc)

- [<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1418">Microsoft Teams 說明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1418">Microsoft Teams help</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/23156c0c-2c6e-49dd-8b7b-7c564b76508c)

### <a name="microsoft-power-automate-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-1577">Microsoft Power Automate 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1577">Microsoft Power Automate activities</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-stream-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-1586">Microsoft Stream 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1586">Microsoft Stream activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1587">您可以在 Microsoft Stream 中搜尋活動的稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1587">You can search the audit log for activities in Microsoft Stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1588">這些活動包括使用者執行的視訊活動、群組頻道活動及系統管理員活動，例如管理使用者、管理組織設定及匯出報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1588">These activities include video activities performed by users, group channel activities, and admin activities such as managing users, managing organization settings, and exporting reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1589">如需這些活動的說明，請參閱 [Microsoft Stream 中的稽核記錄](https://docs.microsoft.com/stream/audit-logs#actions-logged-in-stream) (英文) 中的「Stream 中記錄的動作」一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1589">For a description of these activities, see the "Actions logged in Stream" section in [Audit Logs in Microsoft Stream](https://docs.microsoft.com/stream/audit-logs#actions-logged-in-stream).</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-forms-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-1621">Microsoft Teams 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1621">Microsoft Forms activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1622">下表列出 Office 365 稽核記錄中記錄的 Microsoft Forms 使用者和系統管理員活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1622">The following table lists the user and admin activities in Microsoft Forms that are logged in the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1623">Microsoft Forms 是用來收集資料的表單/測驗/問卷工具，以進行資料分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1623">Microsoft Forms is a forms/quiz/survey tool used to collect data for analysis.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1624">以下說明中指出部分作業包含的其他活動參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1624">Where noted below in the descriptions, some operations contain additional activity parameters.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1625">如果 Forms 活動是由共同作者或匿名回應者執行，則記錄方式會稍有不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1625">If a Forms activity is performed by a co-author or an anonymous responder, it will be logged slightly differently.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1626">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[由共同作者和匿名回應者執行的 Forms 活動](#forms-activities-performed-by-co-authors-and-anonymous-responders)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1626">For more information, see the [Forms activities performed by co-authors and anonymous responders](#forms-activities-performed-by-co-authors-and-anonymous-responders) section.</span></span>

#### <a name="forms-activities-performed-by-co-authors-and-anonymous-responders"></a><span data-ttu-id="078fd-1736">由共同作者和匿名回應者執行的 Forms 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1736">Forms activities performed by co-authors and anonymous responders</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="078fd-1737">在設計表單和分析回應時，Forms 支援共同作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1737">Forms supports collaboration when forms are being designed and when analyzing responses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1738">表單合作者稱為 [共同作者]\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1738">A form collaborator is known as a *co-author*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1739">除了刪除或移動表單以外，共同作者可以執行表單擁有者可以執行的所有動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1739">Co-authors can do everything a form owner can do, except delete or move a form.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1740">Forms 也可讓您建立可匿名回應的表單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1740">Forms also allows you to create a form that can be responded to anonymously.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="078fd-1741">這表示回應者不需要登入您的組織就能回應表單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="078fd-1741">This means the responder doesn't have to be signed into your organization to respond to a form.</span></span>
